<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:портной.html>портно́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">portnój</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:портной.html>портно́го</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:портной.html>портны́е</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:портной.html>портны́х</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:портниха.html>портни́ха</a></b>)

***портовый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:портовый.html>порто́вый</a> (11124)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порт.html>порт</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">port</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о́вый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-óvyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:портовый.html>порто́вый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">portóvyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> port
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:портовый.html>порто́вый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:город.html>го́род</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>portóvyj</b> górod</i> ― <span class="e-translation">seaport</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>port</b> city</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<ol><li>швейцар, привратник</li>
</ol>

***поругаться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поругаться.html>поруга́ться</a> (15896)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поругать.html>поруга́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">porugátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поругаться.html>поруга́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">porugátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to quarrel <i>(with)</i>, to break <i>(off) (with)</i></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поругать.html>поруга́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">porugátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поругать.html>поруга́ть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">porugátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">поруга́ние</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">porugánije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ругать.html>руга́ть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">rugátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выругать.html>вы́ругать</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">výrugatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порука.html>пору́ка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">porúka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порука.html>пору́ки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порука.html>пору́ки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порука.html>пору́к</a></b>)

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отпускать.html>отпуска́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:порука.html>пору́ки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">otpuskátʹ na porúki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to accept bail</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:круговой.html>кругова́я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:порука.html>пору́ка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">krugovája porúka</i> ― <span class="e-translation">mutual responsibility, collective guarantee, cover-up</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поручавший.html>поруча́вший</a> (15355)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поручаться.html>поруча́ться</a> (28031)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поручать.html>поруча́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">poručátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поручать.html>поруча́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">poručátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***поручение.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поручение.html>поруче́ние</a> (4402)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поручать.html>поруча́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">poručátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to commission, to entrust</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ручать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ručatʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to vouch, to guarantee</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>рука́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ruká</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hand</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (see there for more)
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поручение.html>поруче́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poručénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поручение.html>поруче́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поручение.html>поруче́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поручение.html>поруче́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>assignment, commission, errand
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дипломатический.html>дипломати́ческое</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:поручение.html>поруче́ние</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">diplomatíčeskoje <b>poručénije</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">diplomatic mission</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:давать.html>дава́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:поручение.html>поруче́ние</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">davátʹ <b>poručénije</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to charge; to instruct</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:давать.html>дава́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:важный.html>ва́жное</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:поручение.html>поруче́ние</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">davátʹ vážnoje <b>poručénije</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">charge with an important mission</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>да́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>ей</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:поручение.html>поруче́ние</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on dal jej éto <b>poručénije</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">he gave her the commission</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:поручение.html>поруче́нию</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">po <b>poručéniju</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">on the instructions; on a commission; on behalf; per procurationem</span></div></dd>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поручень.html>по́ручень</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">póručenʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поручень.html>по́ручня</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поручень.html>по́ручни</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поручень.html>по́ручней</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>handrail
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:держаться.html>держа́ться</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:поручень.html>по́ручень</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">deržátʹsja za <b>póručenʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">hold the handrail</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***поручиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поручиться.html>поручи́ться</a> (12072)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поручить.html>поручи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">poručítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поручиться.html>поручи́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poručítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ручаться.html>руча́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to warrant, to guarantee, to certify, to answer for, to vouch for <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + accusative, someone/something</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:поручиться.html>поручи́лся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>голово́й</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja <b>poručílsja</b> za éto golovój.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I <b>answered/vouched</b> for it with my life; I staked my life on it.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:поручиться.html>поручу́сь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>то</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> ....</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja <b>Poručúsʹ</b> za to, što ....</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I <b>will guarantee</b> that ....</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfectives:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ручаться.html>руча́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ručátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поручаться.html>поруча́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">poručátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to assure, to promise
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:поручиться.html>поручи́лся</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сделать.html>сде́лаю</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja <b>poručílsja</b>, što sdélaju éto.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I promised I will do it.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to bet, to be sure</li>

***порушить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:порушить.html>пору́шить</a> (22314)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рушить.html>ру́шить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rúšitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порушить.html>пору́шить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">porúšitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to destroy</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to tear down</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to disrupt, to frustrate, to ruin</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">пору́шиться</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">porúšitʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***порхать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:порхать.html>порха́ть</a> (14606)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pьrxati</i>/<i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pъrxati</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порхать.html>порха́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">porxátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">порхну́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to flit, to flutter, to fly about</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">ironical<span class="ib-comma">,</span> deprecative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to hop, to move <i>(from place to place)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:порхать.html>порха́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>одного́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>места</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:работа.html>рабо́ты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:другой.html>друго́е</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>porxátʹ</b> s odnovó mesta rabóty na drugóje</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to job-hop</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:порча.html>по́рча</a> (12865)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Deverbal of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:портить.html>по́ртить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pórtitʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to spoil, damage</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порча.html>по́рча</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pórča</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порча.html>по́рчи</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порча.html>по́рчи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порча.html>по́рч</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>spoiling</li>
<li>damage
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:порча.html>по́рча</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:груз.html>гру́за</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pórča</b> grúza</i> ― <span class="e-translation">cargo damage</span></div></dd>

<li>corruption
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:порча.html>по́рча</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:данный.html>да́нных</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pórča</b> dánnyx</i> ― <span class="e-translation">data corruption</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>evil curse, hex
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наводить.html>наводи́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:портить.html>по́рчу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">navodítʹ pórču</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to put an evil curse; to hex</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***поршень.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:жало.html>поршень</a> (24485)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жало.html>по́ршень</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">póršenʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поршень.html>по́ршня</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поршень.html>по́ршни</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поршень.html>по́ршней</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поршень.html>поршне́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>piston; sucker, plunger</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:порыв.html>поры́в</a> (3911)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Deverbal of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">порыва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">poryvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порыв.html>поры́в</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">porýv</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порыв.html>поры́ва</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порыв.html>поры́вы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порыв.html>поры́вов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>gust <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a strong, abrupt rush of wind</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>fit <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">sudden outburst of emotion</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
